I've created a comprehensive CLI reference document for GitHub Codespaces at `/workspaces/ai-frame/.vibe/docs/codespaces-cli-reference.md`. This document covers:

## Key Sections:

1. **Installation and Setup** - How to install and authenticate with GitHub CLI
2. **Core Commands** - Essential commands for creating, listing, and managing codespaces
3. **Port Forwarding** - Complete port management including visibility settings
4. **Environment Configuration** - Secrets, environment variables, and configuration
5. **Advanced Operations** - File operations, command execution, and configuration
6. **Automation and Scripting** - Bash and Python automation examples
7. **API Access** - Using `gh api` for advanced codespace operations
8. **Troubleshooting** - Common issues and solutions

## Highlights:

### Essential Commands:
- `gh codespace create` - Create new codespaces with specific configurations
- `gh codespace list` - List and filter codespaces
- `gh codespace ports` - Manage port forwarding and visibility
- `gh codespace ssh` - Connect and execute commands
- `gh codespace cp` - Copy files to/from codespaces

### Port Management:
- Setting port visibility (public/org/private)
- Forwarding multiple ports
- Querying port configurations

### Automation Examples:
- Bash scripts for automated management
- Python scripts for complex operations
- GitHub Actions workflows for scheduled maintenance

### API Operations:
- Direct API access using `gh api`
- Managing secrets and configurations
- Billing and usage monitoring

The document provides practical examples, automation scripts, and best practices for managing GitHub Codespaces efficiently from the command line.

● Update(CLAUDE.md)
  ⎿  Updated CLAUDE.md with 60 additions and 4 removals
        76
        77    ## Environment Configuration
        78
        79 -  ### GitHub Codespaces
        80 -  - Services auto-detect Codespaces environment
        81 -  - URLs automatically use public Codespaces domains
        82 -  - **IMPORTANT**: Set ports 8443, 3001, 8080 to PUBLIC for Quest access
        79 +  ### GitHub Codespaces (Recommended Deployment)
        80
        81 +  #### Quick Start
        82 +  ```bash
        83 +  # 1. Start all services (choose option 2 for tmux)
        84 +  cd /workspaces/ai-frame/first-attempt
        85 +  ./run-services.sh
        86 +
        87 +  # 2. Set ports to PUBLIC for Quest access
        88 +  gh codespace ports visibility 8443:public
        89 +  gh codespace ports visibility 3001:public
        90 +  gh codespace ports visibility 8080:public
        91 +
        92 +  # 3. Get Quest launcher URL
        93 +  ./get-launcher-url.sh
        94 +  ```
        95 +
        96 +  #### Environment Variables
        97 +  Codespaces provides these environment variables automatically:
        98 +  ```bash
        99 +  CODESPACES=true                           # Indicates Codespaces environment
       100 +  CODESPACE_NAME=<unique-name>             # e.g., "psychic-spork-r74rr59pp52qxr"
       101 +  GITHUB_CODESPACES_PORT_FORWARDING_DOMAIN=app.github.dev
       102 +  GITHUB_USER=<username>                    # Your GitHub username
       103 +  GITHUB_TOKEN=<token>                      # Auth token for API access
       104 +  ```
       105 +
       106 +  #### URL Structure
       107 +  Services are accessible at:
       108 +  ```
       109 +  https://${CODESPACE_NAME}-${PORT}.${GITHUB_CODESPACES_PORT_FORWARDING_DOMAIN}
       110 +  ```
       111 +
       112 +  Example:
       113 +  - WebXR: `https://psychic-spork-r74rr59pp52qxr-8443.app.github.dev`
       114 +  - API: `https://psychic-spork-r74rr59pp52qxr-3001.app.github.dev`
       115 +
       116 +  #### Command-Line Tools
       117 +  ```bash
       118 +  # Port management
       119 +  gh codespace ports                        # List all forwarded ports
       120 +  gh codespace ports forward 3001:3001     # Forward specific port
       121 +  gh codespace ports visibility 8443:public # Set port visibility
       122 +
       123 +  # Service monitoring
       124 +  tmux ls                                   # List tmux sessions
       125 +  tmux attach -t aiframe                   # Attach to service session
       126 +  tmux kill-session -t aiframe             # Stop all services
       127 +
       128 +  # Debugging
       129 +  curl http://localhost:3001/status        # Check API status
       130 +  lsof -i :8443                            # Check port usage
       131 +  netstat -tlnp | grep 3001                # Network connections
       132 +  ```
       133 +
       134 +  #### Optimal Configuration
       135 +  - **tmux deployment** (option 2) is recommended over Docker for Codespaces
       136 +  - Provides better resource usage and log visibility
       137 +  - Services persist across browser refreshes
       138 +  - Easy individual service restart
       139 +
       140    ### Local Development
       141    - Uses machine's local IP for network access
       142    - Self-signed certificates generated automatically

     1→"""
     2→AI Frame API - FastAPI backend for AR/VR content management
     3→"""
     4→
     5→from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, UploadFile, File, Form, Body
     6→from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
     7→from fastapi.responses import FileResponse, JSONResponse
     8→from fastapi.staticfiles import StaticFiles
     9→from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
    10→from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Any
    11→from datetime import datetime
    12→import json
    13→import os
    14→import uuid
    15→import shutil
    16→from pathlib import Path
    17→import aiofiles
    18→import base64
    19→
    20→# Initialize FastAPI app
    21→app = FastAPI(
    22→    title="AI Frame API",
    23→    description="Backend API for AR/VR object persistence and media management",
    24→    version="1.0.0"
    25→)
    26→
    27→# Configure CORS for browser and XR access
    28→app.add_middleware(
    29→    CORSMiddleware,
    30→    allow_origins=["*"],  # Allow all origins for development
    31→    allow_credentials=True,
    32→    allow_methods=["*"],
    33→    allow_headers=["*"],
    34→    expose_headers=["X-Session-ID"]
    35→)
    36→
    37→# Base directory for data storage
    38→DATA_DIR = Path("/workspaces/ai-frame/data")
    39→DATA_DIR.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    40→
    41→# Mount static files
    42→app.mount("/static", StaticFiles(directory="/workspaces/ai-frame/static"), name="static")
    43→
    44→# ==================== Models ====================
    45→
    46→class Position3D(BaseModel):
    47→    x: float
    48→    y: float
    49→    z: float
    50→
    51→class Rotation3D(BaseModel):
    52→    x: float = 0
    53→    y: float = 0
    54→    z: float = 0
    55→    w: float = 1  # Quaternion
    56→
    57→class ARObject(BaseModel):
    58→    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    59→    type: str  # cube, sphere, cylinder, etc.
    60→    position: Position3D
    61→    rotation: Optional[Rotation3D] = None
    62→    scale: Optional[float] = 1.0
    63→    color: Optional[str] = "#00FF00"
    64→    metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = {}
    65→    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.now)
    66→
    67→class Session(BaseModel):
    68→    id: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: str(uuid.uuid4()))
    69→    name: Optional[str] = None
    70→    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.now)
    71→    updated_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.now)
    72→    objects: List[ARObject] = []
    73→    metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = {}
    74→
    75→class MediaUpload(BaseModel):
    76→    session_id: str
    77→    type: str  # image, video, audio
    78→    filename: str
    79→    metadata: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = {}
    80→    created_at: datetime = Field(default_factory=datetime.now)
    81→
    82→# ==================== Helper Functions ====================
    83→
    84→def get_session_dir(session_id: str) -> Path:
    85→    """Get the directory path for a session"""
    86→    session_dir = DATA_DIR / session_id
    87→    session_dir.mkdir(exist_ok=True)
    88→    return session_dir
    89→
    90→def save_session_data(session_id: str, data: dict):
    91→    """Save session data to JSON file"""
    92→    session_dir = get_session_dir(session_id)
    93→    session_file = session_dir / "session.json"
    94→    with open(session_file, "w") as f:
    95→        json.dump(data, f, indent=2, default=str)
    96→
    97→def load_session_data(session_id: str) -> dict:
    98→    """Load session data from JSON file"""
    99→    session_file = get_session_dir(session_id) / "session.json"
   100→    if not session_file.exists():
   101→        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Session not found")
   102→    with open(session_file, "r") as f:
   103→        return json.load(f)
   104→
   105→# ==================== Session Endpoints ====================
   106→
   107→@app.post("/api/sessions", response_model=Session)
   108→async def create_session(name: Optional[str] = None):
   109→    """Create a new session"""
   110→    session = Session(name=name)
   111→    session_dir = get_session_dir(session.id)
   112→    
   113→    # Create subdirectories for media
   114→    (session_dir / "images").mkdir(exist_ok=True)
   115→    (session_dir / "videos").mkdir(exist_ok=True)
   116→    (session_dir / "audio").mkdir(exist_ok=True)
   117→    (session_dir / "objects").mkdir(exist_ok=True)
   118→    
   119→    # Save initial session data
   120→    save_session_data(session.id, session.dict())
   121→    
   122→    return session
   123→
   124→@app.get("/api/sessions/{session_id}", response_model=Session)
   125→async def get_session(session_id: str):
   126→    """Get session details"""
   127→    data = load_session_data(session_id)
   128→    return Session(**data)
   129→
   130→@app.get("/api/sessions")
   131→async def list_sessions():
   132→    """List all sessions"""
   133→    sessions = []
   134→    for session_dir in DATA_DIR.iterdir():
   135→        if session_dir.is_dir():
   136→            session_file = session_dir / "session.json"
   137→            if session_file.exists():
   138→                with open(session_file, "r") as f:
   139→                    sessions.append(json.load(f))
   140→    return sessions
   141→
   142→@app.delete("/api/sessions/{session_id}")
   143→async def delete_session(session_id: str):
   144→    """Delete a session and all its data"""
   145→    session_dir = get_session_dir(session_id)
   146→    if session_dir.exists():
   147→        shutil.rmtree(session_dir)
   148→        return {"message": "Session deleted successfully"}
   149→    raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Session not found")
   150→
   151→# ==================== Object Endpoints ====================
   152→
   153→@app.post("/api/sessions/{session_id}/objects", response_model=ARObject)
   154→async def add_object(session_id: str, obj: ARObject):
   155→    """Add an object to the session"""
   156→    session_data = load_session_data(session_id)
   157→    
   158→    # Add object to session
   159→    if "objects" not in session_data:
   160→        session_data["objects"] = []
   161→    session_data["objects"].append(obj.dict())
   162→    session_data["updated_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
   163→    
   164→    # Save updated session
   165→    save_session_data(session_id, session_data)
   166→    
   167→    # Also save object separately
   168→    object_file = get_session_dir(session_id) / "objects" / f"{obj.id}.json"
   169→    with open(object_file, "w") as f:
   170→        json.dump(obj.dict(), f, indent=2, default=str)
   171→    
   172→    return obj
   173→
   174→@app.get("/api/sessions/{session_id}/objects")
   175→async def get_objects(session_id: str):
   176→    """Get all objects in a session"""
   177→    session_data = load_session_data(session_id)
   178→    return session_data.get("objects", [])
   179→
   180→@app.get("/api/sessions/{session_id}/objects/{object_id}")
   181→async def get_object(session_id: str, object_id: str):
   182→    """Get a specific object"""
   183→    object_file = get_session_dir(session_id) / "objects" / f"{object_id}.json"
   184→    if not object_file.exists():
   185→        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Object not found")
   186→    with open(object_file, "r") as f:
   187→        return json.load(f)
   188→
   189→@app.put("/api/sessions/{session_id}/objects/{object_id}")
   190→async def update_object(session_id: str, object_id: str, obj: ARObject):
   191→    """Update an object"""
   192→    session_data = load_session_data(session_id)
   193→    
   194→    # Update object in session
   195→    for i, existing_obj in enumerate(session_data.get("objects", [])):
   196→        if existing_obj["id"] == object_id:
   197→            session_data["objects"][i] = obj.dict()
   198→            break
   199→    else:
   200→        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Object not found")
   201→    
   202→    session_data["updated_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
   203→    save_session_data(session_id, session_data)
   204→    
   205→    # Update object file
   206→    object_file = get_session_dir(session_id) / "objects" / f"{object_id}.json"
   207→    with open(object_file, "w") as f:
   208→        json.dump(obj.dict(), f, indent=2, default=str)
   209→    
   210→    return obj
   211→
   212→@app.delete("/api/sessions/{session_id}/objects/{object_id}")
   213→async def delete_object(session_id: str, object_id: str):
   214→    """Delete an object"""
   215→    session_data = load_session_data(session_id)
   216→    
   217→    # Remove from session
   218→    session_data["objects"] = [
   219→        obj for obj in session_data.get("objects", [])
   220→        if obj["id"] != object_id
   221→    ]
   222→    session_data["updated_at"] = datetime.now().isoformat()
   223→    save_session_data(session_id, session_data)
   224→    
   225→    # Delete object file
   226→    object_file = get_session_dir(session_id) / "objects" / f"{object_id}.json"
   227→    if object_file.exists():
   228→        object_file.unlink()
   229→    
   230→    return {"message": "Object deleted successfully"}
   231→
   232→# ==================== Image Endpoints ====================
   233→
   234→@app.post("/api/sessions/{session_id}/images")
   235→async def upload_image(
   236→    session_id: str,
   237→    file: Optional[UploadFile] = File(None),
   238→    image_data: Optional[str] = Form(None),
   239→    metadata: Optional[str] = Form("{}")
   240→):
   241→    """Upload an image (file or base64)"""
   242→    session_dir = get_session_dir(session_id)
   243→    images_dir = session_dir / "images"
   244→    
   245→    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
   246→    
   247→    if file:
   248→        # Handle file upload
   249→        filename = f"{timestamp}_{file.filename}"
   250→        file_path = images_dir / filename
   251→        
   252→        async with aiofiles.open(file_path, "wb") as f:
   253→            content = await file.read()
   254→            await f.write(content)
   255→    elif image_data:
   256→        # Handle base64 data
   257→        filename = f"{timestamp}_capture.png"
   258→        file_path = images_dir / filename
   259→        
   260→        # Remove data URL prefix if present
   261→        if "," in image_data:
   262→            image_data = image_data.split(",")[1]
   263→        
   264→        # Decode and save
   265→        image_bytes = base64.b64decode(image_data)
   266→        async with aiofiles.open(file_path, "wb") as f:
   267→            await f.write(image_bytes)
   268→    else:
   269→        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="No image data provided")
   270→    
   271→    # Save metadata
   272→    meta = json.loads(metadata) if isinstance(metadata, str) else metadata
   273→    meta_file = images_dir / f"{filename}.json"
   274→    with open(meta_file, "w") as f:
   275→        json.dump({
   276→            "filename": filename,
   277→            "created_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
   278→            "metadata": meta
   279→        }, f, indent=2)
   280→    
   281→    return {
   282→        "filename": filename,
   283→        "path": str(file_path),
   284→        "metadata": meta
   285→    }
   286→
   287→@app.get("/api/sessions/{session_id}/images")
   288→async def list_images(session_id: str):
   289→    """List all images in a session"""
   290→    images_dir = get_session_dir(session_id) / "images"
   291→    images = []
   292→    
   293→    for image_file in images_dir.glob("*.png"):
   294→        meta_file = images_dir / f"{image_file.name}.json"
   295→        if meta_file.exists():
   296→            with open(meta_file, "r") as f:
   297→                images.append(json.load(f))
   298→        else:
   299→            images.append({"filename": image_file.name})
   300→    
   301→    for image_file in images_dir.glob("*.jpg"):
   302→        meta_file = images_dir / f"{image_file.name}.json"
   303→        if meta_file.exists():
   304→            with open(meta_file, "r") as f:
   305→                images.append(json.load(f))
   306→        else:
   307→            images.append({"filename": image_file.name})
   308→    
   309→    return images
   310→
   311→@app.get("/api/sessions/{session_id}/images/{filename}")
   312→async def get_image(session_id: str, filename: str):
   313→    """Get an image file"""
   314→    file_path = get_session_dir(session_id) / "images" / filename
   315→    if not file_path.exists():
   316→        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Image not found")
   317→    return FileResponse(file_path)
   318→

   387→# ==================== Audio Endpoints ====================
   388→
   389→@app.post("/api/sessions/{session_id}/audio")
   390→async def upload_audio(
   391→    session_id: str,
   392→    file: Optional[UploadFile] = File(None),
   393→    audio_data: Optional[str] = Form(None),
   394→    metadata: Optional[str] = Form("{}")
   395→):
   396→    """Upload an audio file or base64 data"""
   397→    session_dir = get_session_dir(session_id)
   398→    audio_dir = session_dir / "audio"
   399→    
   400→    timestamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
   401→    
   402→    if file:
   403→        # Handle file upload
   404→        filename = f"{timestamp}_{file.filename}"
   405→        file_path = audio_dir / filename
   406→        
   407→        async with aiofiles.open(file_path, "wb") as f:
   408→            content = await file.read()
   409→            await f.write(content)
   410→    elif audio_data:
   411→        # Handle base64 data
   412→        filename = f"{timestamp}_recording.webm"
   413→        file_path = audio_dir / filename
   414→        
   415→        # Remove data URL prefix if present
   416→        if "," in audio_data:
   417→            audio_data = audio_data.split(",")[1]
   418→        
   419→        # Decode and save
   420→        audio_bytes = base64.b64decode(audio_data)
   421→        async with aiofiles.open(file_path, "wb") as f:
   422→            await f.write(audio_bytes)
   423→    else:
   424→        raise HTTPException(status_code=400, detail="No audio data provided")
   425→    
   426→    # Save metadata
   427→    meta = json.loads(metadata) if isinstance(metadata, str) else metadata
   428→    meta_file = audio_dir / f"{filename}.json"
   429→    with open(meta_file, "w") as f:
   430→        json.dump({
   431→            "filename": filename,
   432→            "created_at": datetime.now().isoformat(),
   433→            "metadata": meta
   434→        }, f, indent=2)
   435→    
   436→    return {
   437→        "filename": filename,
   438→        "path": str(file_path),
   439→        "metadata": meta
   440→    }
   441→
   442→@app.get("/api/sessions/{session_id}/audio")
   443→async def list_audio(session_id: str):
   444→    """List all audio files in a session"""
   445→    audio_dir = get_session_dir(session_id) / "audio"
   446→    audio_files = []
   447→    
   448→    for audio_file in audio_dir.glob("*"):
   449→        if not audio_file.suffix == ".json":
   450→            meta_file = audio_dir / f"{audio_file.name}.json"
   451→            if meta_file.exists():
   452→                with open(meta_file, "r") as f:
   453→                    audio_files.append(json.load(f))
   454→            else:
   455→                audio_files.append({"filename": audio_file.name})
   456→    
   457→    return audio_files
   458→
   459→@app.get("/api/sessions/{session_id}/audio/{filename}")
   460→async def get_audio(session_id: str, filename: str):
   461→    """Get an audio file"""
   462→    file_path = get_session_dir(session_id) / "audio" / filename
   463→    if not file_path.exists():
   464→        raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Audio file not found")
   465→    return FileResponse(file_path)
   466→
   467→# ==================== Health & Status ====================
   468→
   469→@app.get("/")
   470→async def root():
   471→    """Root endpoint"""
   472→    return {
   473→        "name": "AI Frame API",
   474→        "version": "1.0.0",
   475→        "status": "running",
   476→        "endpoints": {
   477→            "api_docs": "/docs",
   478→            "browser_interface": "/static/index.html",
   479→            "xr_interface": "/static/xr.html"
   480→        }
   481→    }
   482→
   483→@app.get("/api/health")
   484→async def health_check():
   485→    """Health check endpoint"""
   486→    return {
   487→        "status": "healthy",
   488→        "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
   489→        "data_dir": str(DATA_DIR),
   490→        "sessions_count": len(list(DATA_DIR.iterdir()))
   491→    }
   492→
   493→if __name__ == "__main__":
   494→    import uvicorn
   495→    # Detect if running in Codespaces
   496→    codespaces = os.environ.get("CODESPACES") == "true"
   497→    
   498→    if codespaces:
   499→        print(f"Running in GitHub Codespaces")
   500→        print(f"Codespace Name: {os.environ.get('CODESPACE_NAME')}")
   501→        print(f"API will be available at: https://{os.environ.get('CODESPACE_NAME')}-8000.{os.environ.get('GITHUB_CODESPACES_PORT_FORWARDING_DOMAIN', 'app.github.dev')}")
   502→    
   503→    uvicorn.run(app, host="0.0.0.0", port=8000, reload=True)

   126→    """Get session details"""
   127→    data = load_session_data(session_id)

   129→
   130→@app.get("/api/sessions")
   131→async def list_sessions():
   132→    """List all sessions with summary info"""
   133→    sessions = []
   134→    for session_dir in DATA_DIR.iterdir():
   135→        if session_dir.is_dir():
   136→            session_file = session_dir / "session.json"
   137→            if session_file.exists():
   138→                with open(session_file, "r") as f:
   139→                    session_data = json.load(f)
   140→                
   141→                # Add summary info
   142→                objects_dir = session_dir / "objects"
   143→                images_dir = session_dir / "images"
   144→                audio_dir = session_dir / "audio"
   145→                
   146→                session_data["summary"] = {
   147→                    "object_count": len(list(objects_dir.glob("*.json"))) if objects_dir.exists() else 0,
   148→                    "image_count": len([f for f in images_dir.glob("*") if not f.suffix == ".json"]) if images_dir.exists() else 0,
   149→                    "audio_count": len([f for f in audio_dir.glob("*") if not f.suffix == ".json"]) if audio_dir.exists() else 0,
   150→                    "display_name": session_data.get("name") or f"Session {session_data['id'][:8]}..."
   151→                }
   152→                
   153→                sessions.append(session_data)
   154→    
   155→    # Sort by created_at, newest first
   156→    sessions.sort(key=lambda x: x.get("created_at", ""), reverse=True)
   157→    return sessions
   158→

   497→        async function initializeSession() {
   498→            try {
   499→                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/sessions`, {
   500→                    method: 'POST',
   501→                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
   502→                    body: JSON.stringify({ name: 'Browser Session ' + new Date().toLocaleString() })
   503→                });
   504→
   505→                if (response.ok) {
   506→                    const session = await response.json();
   507→                    sessionId = session.id;
   508→                    document.getElementById('sessionId').textContent = sessionId.substring(0, 8) + '...';
   509→                    document.getElementById('connectionStatus').textContent = 'Connected';
   510→                    document.getElementById('connectionStatus').style.color = 'green';
   511→                    showStatus('New session created', 'success');
   512→                    
   513→                    // Clear the 3D scene
   514→                    clearScene();
   515→                    objects = [];
   516→                    updateObjectsList();
   517→                    
   518→                    // Refresh session list
   519→                    loadSessionList();
   520→                }
   521→            } catch (error) {
   522→                showStatus('Failed to initialize session: ' + error.message, 'error');
   523→            }
   524→        }
   525→        
   526→        async function loadSessionList() {
   527→            try {
   528→                const response = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/sessions`);
   529→                if (response.ok) {
   530→                    const sessions = await response.json();
   531→                    const dropdown = document.getElementById('sessionDropdown');
   532→                    
   533→                    // Clear existing options except the first one
   534→                    dropdown.innerHTML = '<option value="">-- Select a session to load --</option>';
   535→                    
   536→                    sessions.forEach(session => {
   537→                        const option = document.createElement('option');
   538→                        option.value = session.id;
   539→                        const summary = session.summary || {};
   540→                        const timestamp = new Date(session.created_at).toLocaleString();
   541→                        option.textContent = `${summary.display_name} (${summary.object_count || 0} objects, ${summary.image_count || 0} images) - ${timestamp}`;
   542→                        
   543→                        // Mark current session
   544→                        if (session.id === sessionId) {
   545→                            option.textContent = '✓ ' + option.textContent;
   546→                            option.style.fontWeight = 'bold';
   547→                        }
   548→                        
   549→                        dropdown.appendChild(option);
   550→                    });
   551→                }
   552→            } catch (error) {
   553→                console.error('Failed to load sessions:', error);
   554→            }
   555→        }
   556→        
   557→        async function loadSession(loadSessionId) {
   558→            if (!loadSessionId) return;
   559→            
   560→            try {
   561→                // Get session details
   562→                const sessionResponse = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/sessions/${loadSessionId}`);
   563→                if (!sessionResponse.ok) throw new Error('Session not found');
   564→                
   565→                const session = await sessionResponse.json();
   566→                
   567→                // Get objects for this session
   568→                const objectsResponse = await fetch(`${API_BASE}/api/sessions/${loadSessionId}/objects`);
   569→                if (!objectsResponse.ok) throw new Error('Failed to load objects');
   570→                
   571→                const loadedObjects = await objectsResponse.json();
   572→                
   573→                // Clear current scene
   574→                clearScene();
   575→                
   576→                // Set new session
   577→                sessionId = loadSessionId;
   578→                objects = loadedObjects;
   579→                
   580→                // Add objects to 3D scene
   581→                loadedObjects.forEach(obj => {
   582→                    addObjectToThreeJS(obj);
   583→                });
   584→                
   585→                // Update UI
   586→                document.getElementById('sessionId').textContent = sessionId.substring(0, 8) + '...';
   587→                document.getElementById('connectionStatus').textContent = 'Connected';
   588→                document.getElementById('connectionStatus').style.color = 'green';
   589→                updateObjectsList();
   590→                
   591→                showStatus(`Loaded session with ${loadedObjects.length} objects`, 'success');
   592→                
   593→                // Reset dropdown
   594→                document.getElementById('sessionDropdown').value = '';
   595→                document.getElementById('loadSessionBtn').disabled = true;
   596→                
   597→                // Refresh list to show current session
   598→                loadSessionList();
   599→            } catch (error) {
   600→                showStatus('Failed to load session: ' + error.message, 'error');
   601→            }
   602→        }
   603→        
   604→        function clearScene() {
   605→            if (!scene) return;
   606→            
   607→            // Remove all meshes except lights and grid
   608→            const toRemove = [];
   609→            scene.traverse((child) => {
   610→                if (child.type === 'Mesh' && child.userData && child.userData.id) {
   611→                    toRemove.push(child);
   612→                }
   613→            });
   614→            
   615→            toRemove.forEach(mesh => scene.remove(mesh));
   616→        }
   617→        
   618→        function addObjectToThreeJS(objectData) {
   619→            if (!scene) return;
   620→            
   621→            let geometry;
   622→            switch (objectData.type) {
   623→                case 'cube':
   624→                    geometry = new THREE.BoxGeometry(1, 1, 1);
   625→                    break;
   626→                case 'sphere':
   627→                    geometry = new THREE.SphereGeometry(0.5, 32, 16);
   628→                    break;
   629→                case 'cylinder':
   630→                    geometry = new THREE.CylinderGeometry(0.5, 0.5, 1, 32);
   631→                    break;
   632→                case 'pyramid':
   633→                    geometry = new THREE.ConeGeometry(0.5, 1, 4);
   634→                    break;
   635→                case 'torus':
   636→                    geometry = new THREE.TorusGeometry(0.5, 0.2, 16, 100);
   637→                    break;
   638→                case 'plane':
   639→                    geometry = new THREE.PlaneGeometry(1, 1);
   640→                    break;
   641→                default:
   642→                    geometry = new THREE.BoxGeometry(1, 1, 1);
   643→            }
   644→            
   645→            const material = new THREE.MeshPhongMaterial({ color: objectData.color || '#00FF00' });
   646→            const mesh = new THREE.Mesh(geometry, material);
   647→            
   648→            if (objectData.position) {
   649→                mesh.position.set(objectData.position.x, objectData.position.y, objectData.position.z);
   650→            }
   651→            
   652→            if (objectData.rotation) {
   653→                mesh.quaternion.set(objectData.rotation.x, objectData.rotation.y, objectData.rotation.z, objectData.rotation.w);
   654→            }
   655→            
   656→            if (objectData.scale) {
   657→                mesh.scale.setScalar(objectData.scale);
   658→            }
   659→            
   660→            mesh.userData = objectData;
   661→            scene.add(mesh);
   662→        }

   666→
